<review>This place makes good frozen yogurt, and I absolutely love their non dairy options. Strawberry almond milk tastes delicious! The snacks are hit or miss but when they're a hit they're really tasty. The tofu musubi is my favorite item on the menu. The reason I gave a 3 star rating is that their milk tea has been subpar every time I've gone there, which I don't think should be the case since most of their menu is centered around milk tea. I recently ordered a Dark Roast Oolong Milk Tea with boba pearls, 50% sweetness, and with soy milk. When I drank it, I was immediately met with disappointment. I wasn't sure what I was drinking, but it definitely was not milk tea. It tasted more like watered down almond milk with tea essence sprinkled in. Not tea leaves, but very faint tea essence. And I couldn't tell you what type of tea essence it was because it honestly tasted like nothing. Of course, I ordered 50% sweetness, but I feel like if the tea and milk are good enough quality and mixed right the sweetness should not be what makes or breaks the drink. Additionally, the boba pearls were terrible. They were stale and flavorless. I literally spat out the ones I tasted because they were so unappetizing in my mouth. Cuppa is a really cute place that has an awesome variety of food and drink options, but they seriously need to get it together when it comes to their drinks.< /review>< user_id>

I ordered a used wine red Epiphone Les Paul PlusTop Pro from guitar center and have been let down tremendously. I called to ask about the condition of the guitar, and was told that yes, it had some blemishes, but that the electronics in the  guitar was in great working condition, and that they would have it set up before it was shipped out. To my dismay, I‚Äôve just not received a quality product, and feel as though I was led to believe this product was something that it was not.

1) Long shipping time. Understandable with COVID-19, but they did take 3 weeks when the time was listed as 3-5 days.

2) Original ad said it included a case. No case was delivered

3) Upon opening, notice cosmetic damage is much worse than anticipated. The original picture was taken in a way that the lighting obscured most of the major scratching of the finish.

4) I asked that the guitar be set up before it shipped, and the woman on the phone obliged. However, when I received it, there‚Äôs major fret buzz on the low E string that would require maintenance to fix.

5) I was told that the electronic hardware was all good and ready. Upon receiving, the audio out jack was loose, and the cord must be held in a specific position to keep the connection to the amp from cutting in and out.

6) The pickup toggle is loose, and instead of just having 3 positions, the middle position allows the toggle to move back and forth as though it‚Äôs been broken before.

Overall, I feel like I was led on to believe that this guitar was in good condition all except for some cosmetic damage. If that were the case, I would be far less frustrated, but the fact that the electronics were not in perfect condition tells me that Guitar Center doesn‚Äôt actually care to refurbish or improve damaged materials they buy for resale. It shows me a lack of effort in taking care of used materials, and it‚Äôs really disappointing as a brand new guitarist to receive something that is so beat up without realizing that‚Äôs what I was getting into. Definitely shopping elsewhere in the future.<//text>

< review>
Everything about our hot air balloon adventure was absolutely top rate.  With our friends coming all the way from United Arab Emirates there were challenging schedule issues that Sky Drifters accommodated.  The preflight briefing was thorough and made us all very comfortable with the high level of safety they maintain.  The balloon basket itself was a great size for us.  Not too crowded but not immense like a cattle car.  A bonus was the swinging door that allowed us to walk in rather than having to climb over the rail.

The flight itself was spectacular.  Watching the sun rise over the Sierra Nevada was a postcard perfect moment.  Then we flew over some of California's most beautiful oak grasslands.  Except for no lions or hippos it felt like we could have been over Africa's Serengeti Plain (which is way beyond our budget).

The owner and his wife personally ensured that this was a trip of a lifetime.

Jonas Minton< /review>

<name>Evelynn Chiu</name><Rating>3< /Rating>< Text>
We ordered a Philly Cheese Steak sandwich and it was pretty good, but it wasn't anything that blew us away. The fries were fresh and crispy even though we went late in the evening. I would definitely get the sandwich again, but I'm more excited to try one of their burgers. Hopefully they will prove to be above average!

Because this place isn't super amazing, I feel like the price is a little on the pricier side which makes me a little reluctant to frequent here. I mean, why not go elsewhere where there is cheaper and better food, right?

Service was good once we got someone's attention to take our order. Everyone seemed to be busy cleaning the restaurant for closing in the next hour. Restaurant is inviting and spacious with TVs for those who are looking for a place to watch sports. Menu is pretty extensive and so will cater to different cravings.

For now, this place gets a 3-star review. Definitely will update when I go back in the future when I get to try one of their burgers.< /Text>

When I'm in the mood for a generous burger, this is one of my go-to places.  You'll never run out of different types of burgers to try.  All of the food is consistently good.  You can sit inside or outside the restaurant area which is flanked by a well-stocked bar showing the current sports game of the day.  They really won me over when I was with a friend just to have a drink.  One of us ordered an alcoholic drink, the other a hot chocolate.  No charge for the hot chocolate.  Why?  Because they offer them free to the kiddies who are there with their parents.</Text>
